Account by the archaeologist who discovered the remarkable tombs at Vergina in 1977. Chapters treat the Vergina antiquities, the

Ehrenberg,V. 1960. [3mThe Greek State. [0mOxford: Blackwell. 

Although published in 1960, this account of the Greek state remains a standard source for the defining features of the polis as 
well as its structure and functions. A chapter on types of federations is valuable for developments of the fourth century and 
beyond. 

Hansen, M. H. 2005. [3mThe Shotgun Method: The Demography of the Classical Polis. [0mColumbia, MO: University of Missouri Press. 

One of many recent studies of the Greek polis by one of the most productive scholars on the subject, both through his individual 
publications and through the Copenhagen Polis Centre over which he presides.

Deftly and succinctly pictures the nature of the peoples inhabiting the northern extension of the Greek sphere and their

Ellis, J. 1976. [3mPhilip II and Macedonian Imperialism. [0mLondon: Thames and Hudson. 

This treatment of the rise of Macedonian power, especially during the reign of Philip II, stresses the need for an exceptional 
military in order, first, to survive as an independent state and, increasingly, to control hostile neighbors. The author also 
reveals how the existence of such a force would determine future actions on the part of its leaders.

military revolution (362โ336).

Important essay on an essential ingredient of the success of Philip and Alexander.
